6000017 = { # Théoden Thengling
	name = Th_eoden
	dynasty = 100
	religion = faith_rohirric
	culture = rohirrim
	dna = theoden_dna
	
	father = 6000016
	mother = 6000022
	
	trait = education_martial_4
	trait = brave
	trait = compassionate
	trait = gregarious
	trait = cavalry_leader
	trait = lifestyle_blademaster
	trait = widowed
	disallow_random_traits = yes
	
	martial = 10
	prowess = 7
	diplomacy = 8
	intrigue = 3
	stewardship = 9
	learning = 7
	
	fertility = 0
	sexuality = heterosexual
	
	6981.9.19 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
            add_character_flag = ai_immune_to_mental_breaks
			add_character_flag = immune_to_disease
			add_character_flag = theoden_king
			learn_language = language_westron
			learn_language = language_sindarin
			start_warhorse_story_cycle_effect = yes
			random_owned_story = {
				limit = { story_type = story_cycle_martial_lifestyle_warhorse }
				assign_horse_gender_effect = { GENDER = male }
			}
		}
	}
    6986.3.7 = {
		create_character_memory = {
            type = relative_died			
            participants = {
                dead_relation = character:6000015 #Fengel
            }
        }
	}
	7005.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = theodenswife
        effect = {
			create_character_memory = {
				type = married			
				participants = {
					spouse = character:theodenswife
				}
			}
			add_trait_xp = {
				trait = lifestyle_blademaster
				value = 100
		   }
		}
	}
    7011.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			create_character_memory = {
				type = first_born			
				participants = {
					child = character:6000034 #Theodred
				}
			}
            create_character_memory = {
				type = spouse_died			
				participants = {
					dead_relation = character:theodenswife
				}
			}
		}				
	}
    7013.5.14 = {
		create_character_memory = {
            type = relative_died			
            participants = {
                dead_relation = character:6000016 #Thengel
            }
        }
	}
    7032.1.1 = {
		create_character_memory = {
            type = relative_died			
            participants = {
                dead_relation = character:dolamroth33
            }
        }
		effect = {
			appoint_court_position = {
				recipient = character:6000034
				court_position = second_marshal_of_rohan_position
			}
			appoint_court_position = {
				recipient = character:6000033
				court_position = third_marshal_of_rohan_position
			}
		}
	}
	7052.3.15 = {
		death = { death_reason = death_battle }	#Battle of the Pelennor Fields
	}
}
